The remedy for Capsaicin is oil, its as effective as a true antidote. And it still appears to be an unknown secret. Its like magic. Capsaicin is lipophilic, meaning its attracted to oil (lipids). The oil will draw the Capsaicin out of the skin and hold on to it, relieving the pain almost instantly. When its exterior and/or in your eyes pour oil on and then remove the excess oil with paper towels then rinse using a dish detergent liquid and warm water to remove oil. The dish detergent is specifically designed to cut through oil and will handle that much oil the best. Never use water to try and flush Capsaicin from your eyes, because its lipophilic and attracted to oil it naturally means its repelled by water. ie. the Capsaicin just pushes the water away and is completely useless in washing it off. You can use any oil, olive, veg, flaxseed, castor etc.
